        /**

         * Remove Nulls return '' || underfined || obj

         */

        function removeNulls(obj) {

            if (typeof obj === 'undefined') {

                return undefined;

            }

            if (obj === null) {

                return '';

            }

            if (typeof obj === 'object') {

                for (let key in obj) {

                    obj[key] = removeNulls(obj[key]);

                }

            }

            return obj;

        }



        function searchProductDataById(id, arrayProduct) {

            for (let i in arrayProduct) {

                for (let k in arrayProduct[i]) {

                    if (k == id) {

                        return arrayProduct[i][k];

                    }

                }

            }

            return null;

        }



        function getValuesFromArray(array) {

            let arrayValues = [];

            for (let i in array) {

                for (let k in array[i]) {

                    if (!isNaN(k)) {

                        arrayValues.push(array[i][k]);

                    }

                }

            }

            return arrayValues;

        }



        function removeEvent(obj, value) {

            for (var index in obj) {

                if (obj[index].hasOwnProperty('event') && obj[index]['event'] == value) {

                    delete obj[index];

                }

            }

        }

        function checkEventExists(event) {

            for (let index in dataLayer) {

                if (dataLayer.hasOwnProperty(index)

                    && dataLayer[index].hasOwnProperty('event')

                    && dataLayer[index]['event'] === event

                ) {

                    return true;

                }

            }

            return false;

        }



        window.onpopstate = function (event) {

            if (window.location.href.indexOf('#shipping') > 0 && !checkEventExists('checkout2')) {

                checkout1Page();

            } else if (window.location.href.indexOf('#payment') > 0 && !checkEventExists('checkout2')) {

                checkoutPage2();

            }

        };



        /**

         * Tracking for checkout shipping

         */



        var onePageCheckoutStores = ["de", "uk", "cac_en", "ch_de", "eg_en", "fr", "cl", "mx", "pe"];

        var isSuccessPage = window.location.href.indexOf('/checkout/onepage/success') > 0 || window.location.href.indexOf('/banktransfer/page/success') > 0;

        var isCartPage = window.location.href.indexOf('/checkout/cart') > 0;

        var isCheckoutPage = window.location.href.indexOf('/checkout/') > 0 && !isCartPage;

        var isShippingPage = window.location.href.indexOf('/checkout/#shipping') > 0;

        var isPaymentPage = window.location.href.indexOf('/checkout/#payment') > 0;

        var isFailurePage = window.location.href.indexOf('/checkout/onepage/failure') > 0;

        var isEnhancedPurchase = "0";



        if (isCartPage) {

            setCookieGa('checkout1', false);

            setCookieGa('checkout2', false);

            setCookieGa('checkout21', false);

        }

        if (isSuccessPage) {

            setCookieGa('_dl', false);

            if (isEnhancedPurchase == 1) {

                successPageEnhanced();

            } else {

                successPage();

            }

        } else {

            var storeCode = "vn";

            if (isShippingPage || (onePageCheckoutStores.includes(storeCode) && isCheckoutPage && !isFailurePage)) {

                checkout1Page();

            } else if (isPaymentPage) {

                checkoutPage2();

            }

        }



        

        function getCookieGa(cname) {

            let name = cname + "=";

            let decodedCookie = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie);

            let ca = decodedCookie.split(';');

            for (let i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {

                let c = ca[i];

                while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {

                    c = c.substring(1);

                }

                if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {

                    return c.substring(name.length, c.length);

                }

            }

            return '';

        }



        

        function setCookieGa(cname, cvalue) {

            const d = new Date();

            d.setTime(d.getTime() + 1800000);

            let expires = 'expires=' + d.toUTCString();

            document.cookie = cname + '=' + cvalue + ';' + expires + ';path=/';

        }</script>

  <script type="text/javascript">

        //<![CDATA[

        require([

            'jquery',

            'mage/cookies'

        ], function ($) {

            "use strict";



            var referConfig = {"cookieName":"mp_refer","prefix":"code","isUrlParam":true,"defaultReferUrl":false};

            var value;

            if (referConfig.isUrlParam) {

                var url = new URL(window.location);

                value = url.searchParams.get(referConfig.prefix);

            } else {

                value = window.location.hash;

                if (value) {

                    if (referConfig.prefix && (value.indexOf(referConfig.prefix) !== -1)) {

                        value = value.substr(referConfig.prefix.length + 1)

                    } else {

                        value = value.substr(1);

                    }

                }

            }



            setCookie(value, referConfig);



            function setCookie(value, referConfig) {

                if (value) {

        function setCookieLocalTime() {

            var currentTime = new Date();

            var hours = currentTime.getHours();

            var minutes = currentTime.getMinutes();

            var year = currentTime.getFullYear();

            var mouth = currentTime.getMonth() + 1;

            var date = currentTime.getDate();

            var sec = currentTime.getSeconds();



            var suffix = "AM";



            if (hours >= 12) {

                suffix = "PM";

                hours;

            }



            if (hours == 0) {

                hours = 12;

            }



            if (minutes < 10) {

                minutes = "0" + minutes;

            }



            if (sec < 10) {

                sec = "0" + sec;

            }



            

            const tz = Intl.DateTimeFormat().resolvedOptions().timeZone;



            currentTime.setTime(currentTime.getTime()+(60*1000));

            document.cookie="time_client_date="+year+"-"+mouth+"-"+date+" "+hours +":"+minutes+":"+ sec +";path=/";

            document.cookie="time_zone_client="+tz +";path=/";

        }</script>
